Manually.\n\n\n\nHow is impact others inside and outside my function? No impact.\n\n\n\nWhat changes would this RFE bring to our workflows? Save time and increase\n\nefficiency.\n\n\n\nRate the level of impact to acQuire business\n\n\n\n(if applicable)\n\n\n\n1: Minimal, customer will continue to buy\n\n\n\nCan you quantify the impact:\n\n\n\nAnnual Maintenance value: \n\n\n\nNone \n\n\n\nWorkaround(s)\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n[Implication]\n\n\n\nManual method\n\n\n\nAdditional Comments\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nv4.1\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n\n\nUser Story Creation Guide - Please Read\n\n\n\n\n\nGoals\n\n\n\n\n\n1.       Implementation and Technology Agnostic (within practicality)\n\n\n\n2.       Provides Context, a reason and cause for the user engaging in\n\nthe activity\n\n\n\n3.       Details a sufficient amount of information as to allow a\n\ndeveloper to code against it and a tester to test against it.\n\n\n\n\n\nRules of Thumb\n\n\n\n\n\n·       Balanced: Avoid doing exactly what the user asks for and avoid\n\ndeciding you know better than the user.\n\n\n\n·       Complete Story: \n\n\n\no   Who: is always only one person\n\n\n\no   What: is always only one thing they want to achieve \n\n\n\no   Why: why this outcome matters to the user.\n\n\n\n·       Acceptance Criteria: a clearly expressing a user\x19 s expected\n\nexperience from and action\n\n\n\n·       Visualized: When in doubt write out like a movie of comic book\n\nstrip. If you cannot draw it based on your description, a developer\n\ncannot develop it based on that description.\n\n\n\n·       Apportioned: When in doubt make it an Epic. (Each feature\n\nshould have an epic).\n\n\n\n\n\nI.N.V.E.S.T\n\n\n\n\n\n·       Independent: means it describes the whole process from cause of\n\ndesire to outcome\n\n\n\n·       Negotiable: Keep the details of the ticket something\n\ndiscussable with a developer, do not specify what actions a developer\n\nmust take, only what they must achieve.\n\n\n\n·       Valuable: There should be a defined relatable value to the user\n\n/ purchaser. A clear reason for engaging in the activity, understandable\n\nby almost anyone.\n\n\n\n·       Estimable: The story should be enough that a developer could\n\nunderstand all the things that must be done in order to realise the\n\noutcome for the user and list them.\n\n\n\n·       Small: each story should detail only one interaction with the\n\nproduct.\n\n\n\n·       Testable: ensure enough detail on how the \x1c who\x1d  would know if\n\nit worked.\n\n\n\n\n\nTemplate\n\n\n\n\n\nUser Story\n\n\n\n\n\nAs a [Type of User] \n\n\n\nI want to [Action taken]\n\n\n\nSo that [Cause of the action to be taken]\n\n\n\n\n\nAcceptance Criteria\n\n\n\n\n\nGiven [The state of the product]\n\n\n\nWhen [The action taken by the user]\n\n\n\nThen [The expected behaviour of the product]\n\n\n\n\n\nWords to Avoid\n\n\n\n\n\nFast, Seamless, Natural, Obvious, Correct, Appropriate, Logical,\n\nNormal, Common Sense, Intuitive, etc.\n\n\n\nIf you cannot draw it based on that word, a developer cannot develop it\n\nbased on that word.\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n\n\nFaraz Ahmed ACP GDT\t\n\nGeoscientific Data Technologist\t\n\nacQuire Technology Solutions Pty Ltd\t\n\nT: \t+61 8 9316 6600 <tel:+61%208%209316%206600> \t\n\nF: \t+61 8 9316 6699 <tel:+61%208%209316%206699> \t\n\nE: \tf.ahmed@acquire.com.au <mailto:f.ahmed@acquire.com.au> \t\n\nW: \twww.acquire.com.au <http://www.acquire.com.au> \t\n\n26 Kintail Road, Applecross, Western Australia 6153 | PO Box 933,\n\nCanning Bridge, Western Australia 6153 <http://www.acquire.com.au> \t\n\nAUSTRALIA | CANADA | CHILE | SOUTH AFRICA\t\n\nGIM Suite Practitioner (2000) Brisbane - September 12th to 15th, 2017\n\nGIM Suite Starter (1000) Brisbane - October 25th to 27th, 2017\n\nAdvanced SQL, Script Objects and Data Tracking (400) Brisbane -\n\nNovember 20th to 24th, 2017\t\n\nThis email (including all attachments) is the sole property of acQuire\n\nTechnology Solutions Pty Ltd and may be confidential.
